//\\t\\\"/{name}\\\"                 \\\"\\\"\\n252: //\\t\\\"/{name}/scale\\\"           \\\"scale\\\"\\n253: //\\t\\\"/{name}/scale/foo\\\"       invalid input\\n254: func subresource(path string) subresource(path)\\n283: \\tif len(sub) > 0 {\\n284: \\t\\tsub = \\\" \\\" + sub + \\\" of\\\"\\n285: \\t}\\n286: \\tswitch operationVerb {\\n287: \\tcase \\\"patch\\\":\\n288: \\t\\tdescription = \\\"partially update\\\" + sub + article + b.kind\\n289: \\tcase \\\"deletecollection\\\":\\n290: \\t\\t// to match the text for built-in APIs\\n291: \\t\\tif len(sub) > 0 {\\n292: \\t\\t\\tsub = sub server.\\n\\n### 1. CRD Validation Spec (Input)\\n\\nThe process starts with a CustomResourceDefinition (CRD) object defined in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/v1/types.go`. Each CRD has:\\n- A `Spec.Validation` field of type `CustomResourceValidation`\\n- Which contains an `OpenAPIV3Schema` field of type `JSONSchemaProps` (OpenAPI schema definition)\\n- Additional fields for defining validation rules via `XValidations`\\n\\n### 2. Structural Schema Extraction\\n\\nThe key conversion happens in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/convert.go`:\\n\\n**NewStructural()** function:\\n- Takes `JSONSchemaProps` (the CRD's validation schema) as input\\n- Converts it to an internal `Structural` schema representation\\n- Extracts:\\n  - Type information\\n  - Properties and additionalProperties\\n  - Items (array element schema)\\n  - Validation constraints (format, pattern, min/max values, etc.)\\n  - Kubernetes-specific extensions (x-kubernetes-list-type, x-kubernetes-preserve-unknown-fields, etc.)\\n  - Validation extensions (x-kubernetes-validations for CEL rules)\\n- Recursively processes nested properties and items\\n\\nThe `Structural` type is defined in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/structural.go` and serves as an intermediate representation optimized for validation and OpenAPI generation.\\n\\n### 3. CRD Controllers that Manage OpenAPI Updates\\n\\nTwo controllers watch CRD changes and rebuild OpenAPI specs:\\n\\n**OpenAPI v2 Controller** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/controller/openapi/controller.go`):\\n- Watches all CRDs via informer\\n- For each CRD, builds OpenAPI v2 specs for all served versions\\n- Merges all CRD specs together with the static API server spec\\n- Updates `handler.OpenAPIService` via `UpdateSpecLazy()`\\n- Publishes merged spec at `/openapi/v2`\\n\\n**OpenAPI v3 Controller** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/controller/openapiv3/controller.go`):\\n- Watches all CRDs via informer\\n- For each CRD version, calls `buildV3Spec()` which invokes `BuildOpenAPIV3()`\\n- Stores specs organized by GroupVersion\\n- Updates `handler3.OpenAPIService.UpdateGroupVersion()` with built specs\\n- Publishes specs at `/openapi/v3/<group>/<version>`\\n\\nBoth controllers respond to CRD additions, updates, and deletions in real-time.\\n\\n### 5. API Server Endpoint Publication\\n\\n**Routes Installation** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/routes/openapi.go`):\\n- `InstallV2()` function:\\n  - Builds OpenAPI v2 spec from all registered web services\\n  - Creates `handler.OpenAPIService` with the spec\\n  - Registers the service at `/openapi/v2` endpoint\\n  - Prunes default values to keep spec size reasonable\\n\\n- `InstallV3()` function:\\n  - Creates `handler3.OpenAPIService`\\n  - Builds OpenAPI v3 specs per group/version from registered web services\\n  - Updates the service with specs via `UpdateGroupVersion()`\\n  - Registers handlers at `/openapi/v3` endpoint\\n\\n**OpenAPI v3 Handler** (`vendor/k8s.io/kube-openapi/pkg/handler3/handler.go`):\\n- `RegisterOpenAPIV3VersionedService()` method:\\n  - Registers `HandleDiscovery()` handler at `/openapi/v3`\\n  - Registers `HandleGroupVersion()` handler at `/openapi/v3/` with prefix matching\\n\\n- `HandleDiscovery()` method:\\n  - Serves OpenAPI v3 discovery document\\n  - Lists all available group/versions\\n\\n- `HandleGroupVersion()` method:\\n  - Serves the OpenAPI v3 schema for a specific group/version\\n  - Extracts group and version from request URL\\n  - Returns the corresponding schema\\n\\nThe OpenAPI v2 handler in `vendor/k8s.io/kube-openapi/pkg/handler/handler.go` follows a similar pattern, registering at `/openapi/v2`.\\n\\n### 6. Version Conversion\\n\\nFor clients that need OpenAPI v2 specs, the system can convert v3 to v2 using:\\n- `vendor/k8s.io/kube-openapi/pkg/openapiconv/convert.go` - `ConvertV2ToV3()` function\\n-
